			multiply_variable = { 
				var = random_factor 
				value = 0.2
			}
			add_to_variable = { 
				var = random_factor 
				value = -0.1
			}

			add_to_variable = { 
				var = fun_reform_approval_rate 
				value = random_factor
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { 
					var = issue_4_approval
					value = 1
	          		compare = equals
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				var = fun_reform_approval_rate
				value = 0.2
			}

			set_variable = { 
				var = random_factor 
				value = random
			}
			multiply_variable = { 
				var = random_factor 
				value = 0.2
			}
			add_to_variable = { 
				var = random_factor 
				value = -0.1
			}

			add_to_variable = { 
				var = fun_reform_approval_rate 
				value = random_factor
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { 
					var = issue_4_approval
					value = 2
	          		compare = equals
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				var = fun_reform_approval_rate
				value = 0.4
			}

			set_variable = { 
				var = random_factor 
				value = random
			}
			multiply_variable = { 
				var = random_factor 
				value = 0.2
			}
			add_to_variable = { 
				var = random_factor 
				value = -0.1
			}

			add_to_variable = { 
				var = fun_reform_approval_rate 
				value = random_factor
			}
		}
		else = {

		}
	}
}

calculate_reform_vote_results = {
	set_variable = { 
		var = reform_yay_value 
		value = 0
	}

	set_variable = { 
		var = reform_nay_value 
		value = 0
	}

	### VAN_COM VOTES

	set_variable = { 
		var = reform_yay_van_com_value 
		value = parl_van_com_seats_count
	}

	multiply_variable = { 
		var = reform_yay_van_com_value 
		value = van_com_reform_approval_rate
	}

	round_variable = reform_yay_van_com_value

	set_variable = { 
		var = reform_nay_van_com_value 
		value = parl_van_com_seats_count
	}

	subtract_from_variable = { 
		var = reform_nay_van_com_value 
		value = reform_yay_van_com_value
	}

	###

		var = reform_yay_value 
		value = reform_yay_van_com_value

		value = reform_nay_van_com_value

analyse_reform_vote_results = {
	if = {
		limit = { # YAY
			check_variable = { 
				var = reform_yay_value
				value = reform_nay_value
          		compare = greater_than
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = eoanb_reform_vote_success
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { # NAY
			check_variable = { 
				var = reform_nay_value
				value = reform_yay_value
          		compare = greater_than
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = eoanb_reform_vote_failure
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { # TIE
			check_variable = { 
				var = reform_yay_value
				value = reform_nay_value
          		compare = equals
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = eoanb_reform_vote_tie
	}
}
